- Black has pieces at their standard starting positions
- Black's knights are placed actively, with Nf6 already developed
- Black's pawns control the center well
- White's pieces are also at starting positions

**My Strategic Assessment:**
As black, I want to complete my development and fight for control. My knight on f6 is already active and threatens several squares. Let me move it to g4, which is an excellent active square.

**Why Ng4?**
1. **Development**: This develops the second knight efficiently
2. **Attack**: The knight creates threats against f2 and h2
3. **Tension**: It maintains pawn tension and restricts white's kingside
